The current market price is 24 yuan per barrel. Zhenghong Jichanghe has also increased to 27.8 yuan, and Jiyingfeng is 27 yuan. Sales have just started, and they have already shown their edge. If strong sales are encountered, I am afraid there will be even more prospects. White tung oil is steadily rising. Since a foreign company in Hankou sold it at 30 yuan and 4 jiao, fortunately, the subsequent delivery was not strong, and it can be temporarily fixed. If there is a follow-up purchase, it must be added again. Foreign companies in Shanghai also make a small number of purchases, but foreign trade is handled by one or two bean and rice firms, and there are only two or three tung oil firms doing foreign business, and the scope is not as large as bean and rice firms. Therefore, when there is a transaction, only a few dozen tons can be sold, so the inflow and outflow are not large. Recently, it was heard that a certain bean and rice firm had settled a large number and was searching for and handling it in Hangzhou for several days, which stimulated the market. Generally, the price for shipping from Hangzhou to Shanghai must be 37 yuan per block. With such strong foreign demand, it can be said that the market will always have more glory than disgrace.

(Hangzhou Silk Cocoon Brokers Suppressing Prices) Cocoon brokers in Lin'an and other places in Hangzhou have been weighing and collecting cocoons for more than ten days. New cocoons in the four villages have a good harvest, and the market arrival is quite strong. The price of cocoons is not high. At the beginning, the price of improved varieties of high-quality cocoons was 30 yuan per Sima catty, and the price of local varieties was 20 yuan. Recently, silk cocoon merchants have continued to decline in the spot price of silk in Europe and the United States, so they are suppressing prices and collecting cocoons. In the past two days, improved cocoons were only 20 to 25 yuan, and local cocoons were 14 to 18.9 yuan, and farmers suffered losses. (Shaoxing Fresh Cocoons Arrive in Large Quantities) Shaoxing's four villages mostly produce early silkworms, and the harvest is the richest in the late improved varieties of cocoons. The new cocoons have been on the market for more than ten days, and more than ten cocoon shops have opened. The price of cocoons is restricted by public discussion and cannot be allowed to fluctuate. The price of improved varieties is 25 yuan per Sima catty, and the price of local cocoons is 18.5 yuan. The market price is only 20 yuan to 14 yuan, and all silkworm farmers are losing money.

(Nanjing Fresh Cocoons Open at a Low Price) The improved varieties bred in various cities and villages in Nanjing are of excellent quality due to effective guidance, and the cocoon production is quite abundant. However, there are few cocoon shops that have opened, and the price of cocoons is not high. The highest price for improved varieties of high-quality cocoons is only 24.5 yuan, and the price of local varieties is 18.5 yuan, and silkworm farmers cannot afford to make losses.

(Shiying Silkworm Farmers are Selling at a Loss) Farmers in Shiying are breeding silkworms under the guidance of the farm, so they are all leading incubation and breeding. However, the weather is not right, and most of the local silkworms are lost. The improved silkworms incubate quite a bit, eat more leaves, and the cocoon harvest is about 70 to 80% of the year, but the cost is not cheap. The newly opened price of cocoon shops is only 14 yuan (local cocoons) to 20 yuan (improved cocoons).

(Lyon Chinese Silk Prices Report Another Drop) Lyon silk weaving factories are experiencing sluggish sales of silk products, and the use of raw silk has greatly decreased. Japanese merchants are selling new silk at low prices, resulting in another drop in Chinese silk prices. The prices of white factory Jing San Tiaowu brand and other grades are only 58.5 francs per kilo, down 0.5 francs. The prices of Sichuan and Lu yellow factories are over 60 francs, down 1 franc each. Converted to Chinese currency, each package is down 4.5 yuan to 8.9 yuan.

Talking about the Sexual Anxiety of Modern Youth 307

— Peng He

When people reach adolescence, they encounter the problem of sexual anxiety. This sexual anxiety is a major hurdle of adolescence. Of course, sexual needs are not limited to adolescence, but they are most intense during this period. Moreover, sexual anxiety is most dangerous during adolescence. Therefore, many young people often ruin, waste, or even fall because of sexual anxieties. This shows how severely the problem of sexual anxieties is hitting modern youth. Especially in this excessively prosperous city, the atmosphere of the end of the century is full of decadence and wild pleasures. The surrounding negative environment constantly and violently stimulates the minds of every young person, causing everyone to walk down the road to ruin. Sensual movies, legs, cheongsams, alluring prostitutes standing on the side of the road, and extremely sensual dances in movie theaters are all materials that make everyone indulge in decadent and decadent pleasures. Adolescents who are experiencing intense sexual impulses, under this extremely adverse environment, who can resist the temptation and avoid falling? Therefore, in this city, the extent of youthful decadence is particularly serious.

The increasing decadence of young people is particularly regrettable and frightening. Of course, there are many ambitious young people who are willing to bury themselves in hard work, the more adverse the environment is; however, on the other hand, there are also countless weak-willed young people who are buried by the adverse environment, which is a great loss to society.

Why do young people fall into decadence like this? This is because the current society is fundamentally unsuitable for cultivating young people. Of course, on the one hand, it can be said that the more adverse the environment is, the more it can hone heroic and promising young people; however, most young people are ultimately unable to progress due to the particularly bad environment. For example, the countryside is bankrupt, and education is bankrupt, which makes it impossible for young people to study. Consequently, the city is also in decline, which makes it impossible for young people to get jobs. These are all fundamental reasons that make it impossible for young people to progress. In particular, the problem of sexuality is because the current society is in the process of alternating between the old and the new. The old women cannot satisfy them, and the new women have not been produced (even if there are, they are extremely few), and the uneven development of society is due to the remaining strong influence of the old social forces, which makes it impossible for young people to have normal social interactions between men and women. In this way, sexual anxiety can only drive young people to the road of decadence. The sexual anxiety of young people should have a proper release at a certain time, and love is also necessary during adolescence, but the current young people cannot get these, so of course they can only fall. The decadence of modern young people is really made by society, this is a very clear fact.

However, let us not forget that history is created by human beings. The irrationality of society requires us to transform it. Who should bear the responsibility for this transformation? Of course, none other than us young people. Because young people (especially poor young people) are generally more revolutionary. Revolutionary youth are the pioneers of the times. Now, we young people have to shoulder the responsibility of transforming society and advancing history. Young people in front of the times, do not hesitate any more, decadence and enjoyment will only bury your life, now we can only bury our heads and work hard. Only burying our heads and working hard is our true way out today. Naturally, the goal of this hard work should undoubtedly be the general public. Sexual anxiety cannot bury your life, and at the same time, the adverse environment can never be used as an excuse for you to shirk your responsibility. Only the cowardly will say that your decadence is caused by the compulsion of the environment.

After Seeing the Performance of the YC Dramatic Society 308

— Luo Ping

Carrying the early summer evening breeze, I walked into the campus of St. John's University, the old site where the anti-imperialist flames ignited during the May 30th Movement. It has now passed like a dream. Guided by Mr. X, I entered the resplendent and luxurious common room. The play *Father Returns* had already begun on the stage.

It seems unnecessary to explain the story of *Father Returns* here, as it is such a familiar drama. I have seen performances of *Father Returns* four or five times, but it was my first time seeing it performed with Japanese costumes. However, it seems that one need not be so overly faithful to that setting. Not only was the kimono unfamiliar and unsuited to the audience, but it also detracted from the plot. Zong Tai's neat Western suit replaced the tattered cotton robe, and because of his upright posture, Zong Tai looked much younger, which made the final collapse seem abrupt. Zhen Niang not sitting in a chair sewing but standing in the center of the stage talking to Xian Yilang seemed unnatural. After Zong Tai came in, he wasn't offered a seat, and he stood in the center of the stage, puffing out his chest as if he were about to give a speech. The overly luxurious scenery did not help the plot, which was already damaged by the costumes and other elements.

However, the biggest mistake was adding the ending that everyone had cut out. It not only made Xian Yilang's personality contradictory due to "innate nature" (a shortcoming that Liang believed was present in Kikuchi Kan's work), but also diluted the power of the tragedy. Originally, the tragic effect of ending the play with Zhen Niang, Xin Erlang, and younger sister crying out for Xian Yilang and their brother after Zong Tai left the house was very powerful. However, adding the ending here reduced the effect of the play. Of course, the responsibility for this must also be attributed to the slave education system that keeps students locked in prison and out of touch with the outside world. It never allows students to look beyond the prison to see what kind of world exists. The ridiculously feudal view of absolutely prohibiting female students from performing further illustrates the unreasonableness of the slave education system.

The second play, *The Will to Live*, was generally better than *Father Returns*. Although there were still many shortcomings, such as forgetting to hang the mother's portrait, the child's crying being too low, and the servant being portrayed with vulgar humor, several actors performed very well. In particular, Lan Yeshen's firm and somber delivery of the line, "Because my will to live is too strong," struck everyone's hearts. This scene was relatively satisfying, and of course, the fact that the script itself was easier to produce an effect was also a reason for this scene's success.

The third play, "Mei Liang," was far superior to the previous two in terms of actors, scenery, and story. Lan Yeshen's A Qiao, Qin Fuji's A Mao, Wang Baoyuan's moneylender, Feng Jizhong's detective, and Wang Jinsheng's Boss Pan all achieved success due to the suitability of their personalities to their roles. Although there were still flaws, such as A Mao not having his hands bound and the improper placement of Boss Pan's bed, these minor flaws did not detract from the overall success of the play.

However, just as they added the ending to *Father Returns*, which everyone had cut out, they made a big mistake by omitting the ending to *Mei Liang*, which everyone performed. After Boss Pan committed suicide (here he merely fell down), A Qiao and his old wife returned, crying and shouting, "Father, why did you commit suicide? Mr. Zhang has already shown us a way out. Don't you see that our bright future is coming soon?" This would have further enhanced the power of *Mei Liang*, but it was not included here.

I also saw the first performance of the YC Dramatic Society, but the progress from the first to the second performance is amazing. On the one hand, it was due to the increased experience of the actors. At the same time, the enrichment of the content of the script added a lot of success. Of course, it also had many mistakes, but I believe that the members of the YC Dramatic Society have great hope, as long as they keep pace with the trends in the theatrical world outside the prison, experience society more, engage with society more, and are willing to learn and work hard, under a sound guide rather than under the shackles of a slave education system that creates foreign slaves and its appendages.

Returning Home at Night 309

— Luo Jia

I seem too cruel, don't I? The small grass by the roadside is already sweetly asleep. The paved stones are already不堪[unbearable] for the trampling of cattle and sheep. Taking advantage of the hanging of the black curtain of night, they are stretching out their limbs, letting fatigue no longer linger. Yes, then I should lighten my footsteps a little.

Lightly, I walk, alcohol reddening my face. Before my eyes, drifting, drifting, are thousands of black eyeballs, beautiful black eyeballs belonging to a certain woman. In my ears, ringing, ringing, is the laughter with the scent of *Lindera obtusiloba*, also belonging to a certain beautiful woman.

Page 20

These, at tonight's banquet of friends, I have already become familiar with. But now, I am cleaving through the night mist to return. And the black eyeballs, and the laughter with the scent of *Lindera obtusiloba*, bite at my clothes, following, following me, where to?

In the lonely night mist, everything is a little blurred. They don't let you bump into them, but they often make you bump into them. In the drunkenness of alcohol, in the intoxication of black eyeballs and the laughter with the scent of *Lindera obtusiloba*, I grope, I want to find a road, a road I can take to return home.

The road at night should be a place that makes people think of imaginable things. For example, beside the new tomb at the foot of the mountain, there are a few phosphorescent lights flashing. But when I tiptoe forward, there is a beautiful woman there. This woman may even be the unparalleled beauty described by ancient poets. At that time, she will generously throw out captivating glances, and awareness-capturing smiles, and even the language of golden silk nightingales singing. What should I do then? Then I should step forward, embrace, embrace tightly. I close my eyes in intoxication, kiss madly, kiss madly. But suddenly I smell a fishy smell. I open my eyes, and a red-faced, green-faced ghost with a long tongue is being held tightly by me. She laughs, laughs like a collapsing city wall. What can I do?

The road at night is full of fantasy. I know that this kind of encounter is impossible. I know that it is possible to scare the胆[gall], but I am willing to have this one encounter, even if I am dragged into the desolate tomb by the ghost.

But the night is beautiful, tranquil, and not snobbish. It can make a person entangled in mundane affairs forget on the road at night, and it can make you produce all kinds of night road fantasies. He whom you cannot meet in the daytime, whom you cannot dream of in dreams, the night can make you think of on the road at night. In an instant, the night can satisfy you.

The owl's laughter cannot be seen in the daytime, but at night, you can hear it without difficulty, hear the singing of this king of the night.

Returning home at night allows people to appreciate what they have never appreciated on weekdays. Now I have fully and satisfyingly drawn from it, but what spoils my mood is that the lights of my home are already flickering before my eyes.

A corner of Robison Road in western Shanghai fully exposes another side of urban life in the oriental Paris of the universe. Every day at five o'clock in the morning and five o'clock in the afternoon is the busiest time on Robison Road, and all activities begin. This is the artistic appreciation of the laborers, this is the comprehensive art of the masses. The performance of two or three people can attract hundreds of spectators, but unfortunately these are all low-grade tastes, close to vulgarity!

On both sides of the road and at the entrances of the alleys, there are standing open-air gambling stalls, or squatting on the ground, suddenly forming a pile. This is the momentary comfort after twelve hours of imprisonment. They are crowded there, not even easily exhaling a breath, staking what remains in their pockets on a single throw, hoping for victory. The result is that blood and sweat are effortlessly taken from their pockets into someone else's pocket, another layer of exploitation. A cry of "The old man is out!" and they all run away empty-handed.

Suddenly, a burst of "Kill a thousand knives! Cold coffin!" The playful and abusive teasing sounds are the echoes of male workers teasing female workers. Naturally, this is long-term hunger and thirst, not to be considered love, but they do not have the material conditions, unlike the love of modern girls, which is built on material things. Comparing those who ride in rickshaws with those who ride in cars: the former are hardworking, good at operating, and accustomed to enjoying. Night of Battling Mosquitoes 311

— Yin Xiang

"Snap!" The electric light went out quickly.

"Buzz buzz buzz" The mosquitoes began to attack me. I had no mosquito net as a defense, only a thin quilt as a fortress.

"Non-resistanceism!" I sang, really for my own benefit, wanting to sleep peacefully and ignore them, but it wouldn't work. They wanted you to sleep, so they could steal your fresh blood.

"Slap!" I slapped the itchy spot, hitting air, and feeling a large lump of flesh the size of a fingertip, protruding from the skin. Scratch, scratching was still itchy.

"Buzz buzz buzz..." They sang a song of victory in my ears. I reached out in a daze to take off my felt cap as a weapon, and blindly groped in the darkness. The only purpose was to drive them away.

One of their spears pierced my cheek again.

"Slap!" With a casual rub, it was a little wet. One of them had sacrificed, crushed into a mud paste.

"Buzz buzz buzz" Not only did they not retreat, but they sang their military song even louder. I thought, "Maybe they have launched a general offensive... No, not an offensive, just a sneak attack." The wind outside the window howled in the dark world, as if cheering them on.

"Oh... Terrible... night!" I was furious, but without defensive weapons, and in the pitch-black night, I couldn't resist. The only thing I could do was grab a few of their minions to vent my anger.

Pulling up the quilt, I went to sleep, but after a while, my head, hands, and legs slipped out. Their killing sound, "Buzz buzz buzz..." spread everywhere, stealing opportunities, sucking my blood, to enlarge their own bellies. "Slap, slap," I didn't have many hands, taking care of the east but not the west, at most grabbing two, but on my skin, they had built many tomb-like lumps of flesh. The wind blew away the black curtain, and the fish-belly white faintly rose outside the window. I could vaguely see the mosquitoes busily working around my bed, "Buzz buzz..." I dragged out my only weapon again—the felt cap—and hit them hatefully. Blindly groping, wanting to destroy them.

"I should fight, resist," I thought. They were, after all, just petty thieves, not daring to come out openly. At the arrival of dawn, they scattered and hid.

Desert March 312

— Li Ying

Forward, friends! Walk to the end, walk out of this world!

Are you probably thirsty from walking? Do you all eagerly hope to get a drink of water? But there is not a trickle of spring here. Are you probably hungry from walking? Do you all eagerly seek something to eat? But there are no delicious fruits here. This is a world of wind and sand.

But you must always advance, enduring hunger, enduring cold. The wind here howls like a wild beast all day and night, endlessly blowing on you, blowing you up and knocking you down. The sand here covers the sky and the earth like thousands of fists dancing wildly, hitting your head and face, knocking you down and getting up again. This is Satan's world.

But you must always advance, bearing hardship, accepting danger.

Because once you turn back, there will be greater hardships to torment you, deeper dangers to terrorize you. Then, Satan will be completely victorious. He will hide in the dark, watching you, this unfortunate group, with widened eyes and cracked mouths, revealing a triumphant, hideous smile.

Friends, do not hesitate any longer, walk! Throw open your lion-like strides.

Please rub your eyes that are blurred by the wind and sand, and look up at the dragon; at the end, the sun is shining with brilliant light, welcoming you!

But do not forget the trap before your eyes.

Friends! Now is not the time for you to rest. Stand up and walk! May God bless you!

A Thousand Words 313

— Passerby

After reading *Tan Yan*, three huge words are deeply imprinted in my mind—"A Thousand Words." I think about it in the garret, and I think about it on the road. I'm simply obsessed with it. However, it's not love, just three words: "A Thousand Words."

A thousand words, surely I still have them in my stomach, right? As long as I arrange them appropriately, I can go and collect the manuscript fee. All that is required is quality; there are no other requirements. I think, I think, and I can't help but feel happy. Not much is needed, just a thousand words, and the hungry worms in my stomach will no longer cry.

Good, no need to fantasize, hurry up and put the words together. Don't run wild, don't go in circles, just a thousand words and it's done! But, heavens! Although the pen is in my hand, there is not a single word on the page, and my literary inspiration has also taken a leave of absence, no longer in the garret.

Watching the bright white silver dollars and the red and green banknotes being taken away by others, while I, myself, am always scratching my head... what!

Just a thousand words is so difficult. What kind of minds do those who can write ten thousand words at a stroke have? Perhaps they are men of letters, while I am a literary beggar? Since a thousand words is not easy, why do the editors still set a limit? I suppose the world is full of those who write ten thousand words but stray ten thousand miles from the topic, and only I am an exception, so they set this limit, right?

Or perhaps it is precisely because of the limit that I cannot write; if there were no limit, perhaps it would be very easy to write thousands upon thousands of words. Putting down the pen, I can't help but think this way. For the sake of my stomach, for the sake of the manuscript fee, and even more because I cannot write, although I do not dare to cause trouble in the rear, I cannot help but feel a little resentment crawling out of my heart.

In fact, this is my fault. In society, when and where do we not encounter restrictions? Can we do as we please? Are those things that are inconvenient for us not a hundred times more serious than the restriction of a thousand words? Do we not obediently comply with them, daring not to resist or resent them in the slightest? Why fixate on "A Thousand Words" alone!

Moreover, in reality, there is limited space, and there are many who beg for food, how can we let Grandma Wang release her... now the spectators in the world no longer have such a bad habit.

Page 21

They like to eat an economical meal, wanting it to be concise and short.

As for whether an article can be written or not, it has nothing to do with restrictions. Just as someone who knows how to box can still show all their skills even when wearing shackles, someone who does not know how to box cannot produce a single posture or gesture even when their hands and feet are free. It can be seen that whether there is a limit or not is irrelevant.

Thinking this way, I know that I cannot blame others; I can only blame myself for being too stupid to even put together an article of a thousand words, and for letting the hungry worms in my stomach grumble in vain.

For a long time, I stared blankly at the pen, still facing a blank sheet of paper. Only at the beginning of the manuscript paper were there three words written in bold: "A Thousand Words."

Loquat 314

— Fei

The wheels of time are turning forward incessantly, turning. Gusts of gentle breeze have brought the warmth of early summer. Time has mercilessly driven away people's youth. From spring to summer, from summer to winter, the time of a year has passed in just an instant. The short spring light has finally disappeared unnoticed by people!

Another year has passed easily, and it's summer again. The sound of "Crisp and refreshing candied plums..." from the hawkers' mouths has been replaced by the cries of "Mountain loquats." Now that cherry blossoms and plums are out of season, the white sand loquats are following up. Villagers send the loquats into the city by boatload after boatload, and then the hawkers transfer them to the mouths of the eaters, tasting the sour and sweet flavors. Indeed, the people in the city have good fortune with food after all, always eating the latest seasonal goods.

"Silkworms get old and loquats turn yellow!" This saying is most popular in our countryside; I am afraid that even three-year-old children understand it. At present, most of the spring silkworms have already gone to the cocoon frames, so on the loquat mountains, a green shade hangs heavy, revealing the yellow, round, adorable loquats in abundance. There are often three or five children guarding the mountains, unlike the usual quiet, so quiet that even ghosts can be caught.

The loquats are yellow on the mountain, and the cocoons are white on the frame. "This is a beautiful hope that everyone in the village imagines," "Golden footrests in April." Because the great hope of the countryside for the year depends entirely on this one season. Whether yellow or white, they can all be turned into colorful banknotes and snow-white, shiny silver dollars.

My hometown—Dongting Mountain—is originally very famous for its white sand loquats, but unfortunately, most people in Shanghai are not fortunate enough to taste them. Because the so-called mountain loquats they eat are entirely from Tangqi. Tangqi loquats ripen early and look good, and the price is also cheaper, but they taste sour, astringent, and bland. The mountain loquats are not like that. Their ripening period is at least one to two weeks after the Dragon Boat Festival. However, their appearance is not as good as the Tangqi goods, and the price is also more expensive, but the difference is clear once they are tasted. Because they are as sweet as honey and the juice is viscous. But there are also good and bad ones. There are many varieties, the best of the white sand is the green type, followed by the purple type, and then the chuan nao type. In addition to these, there is also a red-haired white sand and a green sweet type, which taste no less than the green type. But people do not recognize the red-haired white sand as white sand, because its style is no different from the red sand. The green sweet type is always green, without any yellow color, so whoever sees it will not want to eat it. There are also many types of red sand, such as early red and falling red.

When I was young, as soon as I saw the loquats on the trees turn a light yellow, a small heart would feel happy. Because, at this time, the silkworm work has ended, and I don't need to go to school, so I spend the whole day on the mountain with a few children, jumping and playing. My mother or sister sends the three meals of the day to the mountain for us to eat. In the evening, I stay on the mountain with my grandmother. Sometimes, I strain my sharp little throat and sing: "Up the mountain, down the mountain, who is stealing loquats? The blind man saw it, the deaf man heard it, the mute told it, the lame man chased it; the wild pheasant on the mountainside, beat the crow, the crow cries wah wah!" After shouting until my mouth is dry, I climb the tree to pick the big, ripe loquats and eat them. I take the peeled skin and the pit and throw them into the tea bushes in one go, because my mother will scold and beat me if she sees it.

Now, whenever I see loquats, I think of my childhood, and at the same time, it also evokes my beautiful, broken dreams!

I rushed into the city in the year I was seventeen, and this year is almost ten years. However, after experiencing several vicissitudes, I am still my old self! Every year, when the loquat season comes, I always feel sad when I see loquats! The scenery of the old place is no longer what it used to be, and my footprints have not been on the loquat mountain for ten years. A flick of the jade leg, ten million in gold!

In the deformed social contradictions of a city, running thousands of miles earns nine copper coins!

The Wet Nurse's Sorrow 315

— Guangyu

It was early summer evening, exactly eight o'clock. In the bedroom of a certain bourgeois family, the violet electric lamp emitted an extremely gentle and clear glow, the colors were the most harmonious.

The owners of the bedroom were a young couple. At that moment, the husband was there, amusing himself by playing a phonograph, and the wife was leaning on the sofa, quietly listening to the lyrics coming from the phonograph. In her hand, she was also holding a collection of modern songs, and her gaze was focused on that song collection.

In the center of the bedroom stood a rocking bed, and sleeping inside was a child about a year old. Needless to say, the child was the crystallization of love of this young couple who owned the bedroom.

There was also a wet nurse. Although she was also young, looking at her haggard face, one would immediately understand that she was an ill-fated woman who had long experienced the sorrows of the world.

At this time, the young master in the rocking bed, having finished sucking his fill of milk, bought with money and forcefully taken from another child, was already fast asleep. Therefore, the wet nurse was ordered by her mistress, under the condition that she shouldn't be idle after eating her fill, to beat her own back and massage the mistress's fair legs.

"The record of the Wet Nurse's Song is really nice to listen to! Darling, put it on and sing it once for me to hear! I can sing along with it!" When the phonograph lyrics finished one song, the mistress turned her face and gave a charming glance to her husband standing beside the machine.

"Really you can sing the Wet Nurse's Song? That's really great."

"Who's fooling you!" the mistress replied, "... well, maybe I don't sing it so well!"

So, the husband began to find the record, and the wife also flipped through the song collection she was holding, page after page, looking for the so-called Wet Nurse's Song lyrics.

| Autumn rain... drips on the phoenix tree... autumn flowers are fully red... |

In this way, the lyrics were finally transmitted from the phonograph, and the wife accompanied them, and the husband raised his left arm to beat time for her.

| Love and... hate... are... heavy... heavy; ... kindness and... hatred... are various... various... |

| The tenth... month of pregnancy the mother's... heart... aches... waaa... a sound... a heroic cry of the child... |

"Darling, your singing voice is extremely beautiful, even more outstanding than the one on the record!" the husband complimented her in this way, but the wife did not make a sound, and kept singing her song.

| Money ah!... breaks apart people... mother and child cannot meet. Class ah!... you send my precious child... away... to the... end... |

| I want... to see... the child's smiling... face, ... I want... to see their sleeping... face. ... |

"Isn't that right? Darling, the child's sleeping face is indeed too adorable!" the husband said, wearing a playful smile and pointing at his own child sleeping in the rocking bed.

The mistress did not stop her singing at all. ... | I want to see my precious child, ... unless in a dream. ... At that time, Zhang the wet nurse, was already hurt deeply in her heart by the phonograph and her mistress's lyrics, and was secretly shedding tears.

"Zhang nanny, why are you crying for no reason?" The husband discovered that Zhang nanny was weeping, and was quite displeased in his heart, so he said sternly.

The mistress also immediately stopped singing, and a layer of sorrow immediately hung on her pink face. Bursting out with rage, she said, "We're so happy, and you just have to come and ruin our luck?"

The mistress's commotion woke the young master in the rocking bed. Zhang nanny hurriedly jumped over and picked him up, holding him in her arms. She put the nipple into his small mouth, and put on a smiling face, acknowledging her mistake to her two young masters, saying, "Good young master, good mistress, I'm not crying! Just now, a strand of silk floated and went into my eye socket, and I couldn't open my eyes for a moment, and tears flowed out. Good young master, good mistress, think, you treat me so well, what else am I dissatisfied with!"

The wise masters, after Zhang nanny's softening explanation, had forgiven her. But from then on, the pitiful Zhang nanny even lost the only remaining right to weep secretly to herself.

Amateur Mailbox

Hoping to Reconcile and Return to Good Terms 316

Editor:

It is embarrassing to say, I am now encountering a marriage problem that I cannot solve. I have long paid attention to your newspaper's mailbox, which is a bright light for society and a guide for youth. I sincerely ask you with utmost sincerity to give me a clear path, and I am waiting with wide eyes, waiting and waiting.

Four or five years ago, my family arranged for me to be engaged to a woman I had never met, which I naturally did not want. Therefore, after meeting a Miss H two years ago, friendship developed into love. Over the course of a year, our passion almost reached the boiling point. At that time, the degree of closeness was truly intimate, with the idea of preferring to be mandarin ducks rather than envying immortals. At the same time, I also noticed that Miss H truly had no insincerity towards me. Who knew that this year, Miss H suddenly became distant from me for some reason and instead became romantically involved with another young man. May I ask, should I continue to pursue Miss H, express my true feelings, and hope to reconcile and return to good terms? Or should I succumb to the old ethics and marry a woman with whom there is no love to speak of? However, Miss H is indeed a rare and exceptional woman. Sir, I implore you to help me resolve this, using it as a compass. With this, I respectfully wish you

Peace　　　　　　　　　Humble person Jiang Sijing respectfully informs you

Answer: She used to love you, but now she is "romantically involved with another young man." That clearly shows that she finds that young man more lovable than you, so she is "distant" from you and close to others. This is not because she has any misunderstanding about you. You want to express your true feelings to her. May I ask, what true feelings do you want to express? Expressing that you sincerely love her may not be able to move her, because she doesn't feel that you don't love her and love someone else instead.

What you should do now is not to "express your true feelings" yourself, but to ask her to "express her true feelings." If she is firm and honestly tells you that she no longer loves you, then you should give up completely. If she says that she has not fallen in love with someone else, then of course it would be best, and you can immediately "reconcile and return to good terms." What is most annoying is if she loves you and also loves someone else. If there is such an indication, you must be cautious. In my opinion, a love triangle is dangerous. If she has such a thought, you must not be sentimental, lest both sides are hurt.

Breaking up with her does not necessarily mean "succumbing to the old ethics." These are completely two different matters. If you are unwilling to marry a "woman with whom there is no love to speak of," you can also not marry after breaking up. I feel that you also have improprieties in this relationship with Miss H. Since you were engaged, how could you become romantically involved with someone else? Even if you are dissatisfied with the engagement, you should maintain chastity during the period the engagement is still valid. Fortunately, you now have a rift with her, otherwise, you would be passionately intimate, but you couldn't get rid of the "country girl." That would be very troublesome. So perhaps her falling in love with someone else is also motivated by the fact that you have not dissolved the original engagement.　　　　　　　　Editor

Fiction

A Letter From Home 317

— Maifu

The candlelight flickered like fireflies, in the silent night, he was silent. His appearance was like this... head down, drooping, just like Johnson deeply repenting at his dead father's ancient book stall. Sorrow, grief, lamentation... like a rope tightly entangling his lonely and wounded heart. His will was shaking like the candlelight before him.

| Should I go back? I've been wandering outside for five whole years, am I going back empty-handed? No, absolutely not! But, what will happen to her frail and helpless heart?... |

Finally, he raised his head, tears falling like beads, and his faint gaze moved to a letter from his homeland, written with blood and tears.

Ping'er:

...Five years since we parted, I have been longing for you every day. In my dreams, I wake up crying. Son, I see your shadow everywhere...

The hometown is no longer the appearance you imagined, it has all changed, it has become so desolate, it is simply heartbreaking...

This heartbreaking thing, this human tragedy, son, I don't want to tell you, but, my son, how can I hide it from you? Alas, your dear little sister Cui, in the first half of the month, in the first half of the month, was sold to human traffickers by her father because of the cold and poverty, for only ten silver dollars. In the hometown, this is a common thing. Your second uncle, this is another unfortunate thing, he became a bandit two months ago, and I heard he was caught, I don't know if he is alive or dead, he was such a gentle and kind person, how could he end up like this, there is no way to avoid it...

Come back! A few dozen dollars is enough, I am looking forward to you day and night beside the door, son, please don't disappoint me...

He cried! He imagined that tragic scene: how Cui sister bid farewell to her parents, and how they made a weeping farewell, how she made her last glimpse of the hometown, a round face smeared with tears, disheveled long hair, ah, how she made her last wail to the world...

His heart shattered like a bomb.

|| Cui sister, your fate is so unfortunate!

He thought of his hometown, a beautiful and secluded mountain village, willows growing all around, a silver-blue winding stream flowing through the village, and every morning several girls would be here washing clothes, singing softly: in the evening, the herdsboys gathered here to water the cattle...

Architecture Special

The Problem of Air Pollution Deserves Attention in Construction Engineering 318

In a metropolis like Shanghai, with a population of over three million and countless factories, the problem of air pollution, especially the smoke emitted from factory chimneys, is unavoidable. However, it seems that those involved in the design, construction, and contracting of construction projects mostly neglect this point. In fact, this is an extremely serious problem that deserves attention. In overseas countries, the issue of Air Pollution is also being studied with great enthusiasm. Now, the reporter will briefly summarize their research findings on the causes of air pollution, the impact of air pollution on buildings, and points to note in design, in three sections as follows:

Causes of Air Pollution

In cities, the biggest cause of air pollution is undoubtedly the uncontrolled emissions from various factory chimneys, as well as fugitive dust, air leaks, brick dust, metal filings, and other weathered particles from various places. These are not present in the air, but gradually mix in, and the air gradually changes from pure to polluted. Since smoke and dust are the main causes of air pollution, the impurities in the pollution can also be imagined. Fuel contains a lot of carbon and a small amount of sulfur. After combustion, the emissions are nothing more than carbon monoxide, carbon dioxide, sulfur dioxide, sulfur trioxide, and other species. In addition, ammonium hydroxide may also be mixed in. These oxides, once hydrated, easily turn into oxygen, such as carbonic acid, such as sulfuric acid, which are the most common pollutants in the air.

Impact of Air Pollution on Buildings After the air is polluted, its impact on buildings can be discussed in terms of water-based materials and steel-based materials. Regarding water-based materials, such as stone, cement, mortar, and cement, etc. They are used in large quantities on the exterior of buildings. If they are polluted by carbon ash and dust, it will impair their appearance, which is not a shallow matter. However, this can still be washed with water. If it is polluted by coal tar sprayed from the chimneys in the air, its adhesiveness will cause it to deeply embed into the pores of the stone, and it will be impossible to remove. After being eroded by tannic acid and other substances in the air, the surface of the building will begin to peel off and will not be as beautiful as before.

Stones such as limestone, marble, and olivine contain more calcium carbonate and are easily corroded; granite, gneiss, and sandstone contain very little and are relatively resistant to damage. Thus, the beauty of the exterior will be almost completely deprived.

Cement and cement-based materials will undergo acidification due to the lime content, resulting in gypsum neoformation. Also this will cause the volume of the aluminum salts contained in them to expand more than three times. This internal swelling force will greatly affect the resistance of the cement and cement-based materials.

Mortar, because it contains too many pores, is affected even more severely.

Regarding steel-based materials, steel, iron, copper, zinc, etc. are used. Their surface is polluted in the same way as water-based materials, and there is also the disadvantage of rust.

Copper and iron are the most easily damaged by polluted air. Although they can be plated with zinc or tin, the damage is even more severe once the coating is broken, and corrosion will follow. (To be continued)

On Sandstone as the Only Material for Building Acid Pools in Acid-Producing Factories 319

In recent years, with the rapid advancement of building materials, almost all previous applications of natural stone blocks as materials have now been replaced by steel, metal, and other man-made materials. Even if they exist, they are only a few or only for decoration purposes. However, it should be known that steel and cement are easily corroded by high-temperature acid liquids, resulting in the weakness of peeling and crumbling, which is not as resistant as natural stone. Therefore, the current trend is that for the construction of acid pools in heavy industrial factories, the material of choice is natural sandstone, because if steel is used for construction, the surface of the steel must be electroplated with a very thick zinc layer to resist corrosion, and if pig iron is used, it must also be protected by enamel. However, the enamel itself is very easy to fall off, so it cannot be used perfectly; as for wood materials, of course, they cannot withstand even a touch of high-temperature strong acid. However, facts and experience have long shown us that stone slabs and strips are more resistant to oxygen corrosion. The key points of various acid-resistant preparations seem to have their own secrets in each area. The only consideration is that sandstone naturally has the ability to resist oxygen corrosion and does not need to be equipped.

Sandstone is one of the sedimentary rocks. Its main component is sand, hence the name sandstone. The rock bed is formed by water, so there are sequences. The rock texture is composed of sand grains of different sizes, so it is inconsistent. The most common silica it contains is quartz (Ouaf), with the rest being iron and others, in addition to very few impurities. Its color ranges from gray, grayish white, to beef color, brown, red, etc., each different due to the dynamic variation in the proportion of minerals contained. The more quartz there is, the lighter the color, and even completely white. If there is more iron, the color gradually deepens. Therefore, the proportion of various substances it contains can be determined by the appearance of the color. The reason why it can resist oxygen is that a large amount of quartz in the minerals it contains can not be corroded by acid. It is known that sandstone with a white color and more quartz is more suitable for this type of acid pool building material, which is one point to pay attention to when selecting materials for construction. In addition, for reliable construction, we can further use a detailed method for chemical analysis, which can obtain more accurate composition. In addition to seeking a large amount of quartz, it is also necessary to seek the absolute absence of iron, otherwise, the iron will be washed away by the acid, and the stone itself will be damaged, which will affect the entire construction. Furthermore, a method of microscopic examination can be used to study in detail the rock texture, crystalline form, and color, which can increase the degree of precision. When the stone inspection is ready and the stone selection is determined, the stone can be quarried, cut into pieces, and construction can begin. The method of construction, the four walls and the bottom, and the shape of the pool, need not be said much. The longer and wider the stone pieces, the better, because more stone seams mean more leaks, which is quite inappropriate. The carving craftsmanship at each joint must be carefully considered, and asbestos can be used as a bonding material to increase the transverse pressure of the acid liquid stored in the water. Steel bars can be hoop around the outer wall of the stone pool to enhance its durability. However, the position of the steel hoops must be one foot or more above the normal maximum acid storage level in the pool to be foolproof.

In addition, there are many points that should be paid attention to in the construction of acid pools. If steam heating pipes are used to increase the temperature of the acid liquid, the material must be chrome-vanadium steel, tungsten-molybdenum steel, codait-molybdenum steel, and other similar alloys to resist oxygen corrosion. Sandstone that contains limestone should never be used, because limestone is easily acidified, which must also be noted.

Heavy industry in China can be said to be still in its infancy. There are only two or three oxygen manufacturing plants. Subsequently, the development of such factories is necessary for industrial development, and the construction of this type of acid pool is also indispensable. Among the three acids, sulfuric, nitric, and hydrochloric, concentrated sulfuric acid is the most severe. Unfortunately, in the past, it was difficult to obtain the best acid-resistant material for building acid pools. I have written this article to share with the public, because our country is vast and rich in resources and has many mountains. Although the production of sandstone is not as high as that of limestone, it cannot be said that it is insufficient for future industrial development. I hope that the construction industry will pay attention to this.

New Rural Architecture (Part II) 320

— Zhongqin

Storage room, this is a room that must be equipped in rural buildings, because in the countryside, the most important thing is the so-called "autumn harvest and winter storage". Storing food is the most important issue, and the life of farmers is entirely tied to this storage work. In rural buildings in European and American countries, the most important room is also the storage room. In the storage room, protection is particularly meticulous, and the lifeline of a farmer's family lies entirely here. The periphery of the storage room is generally arranged to make storage more convenient, without any obstacles, and after storing items, it can be closed tightly to prevent insects and other things from entering. Storage in European and American countries is mainly wheat, and storage in our country is mainly rice, so the storage is the same, and when equipping this storage room, one should consider the size of the items that this family wants to store, otherwise, there may be too little or too much space, causing farmers to not be very welcome to this storage room. As for the old-fashioned granary equipment, that is no longer suitable for current use.

In addition to the storage room, there is the residence. The residence does not need to be built as a multi-story building. Of course, it is not suitable for farmers to build multi-story houses under their economic conditions, but hygiene must be taken into account when building, so that there will be no difficult health problems for farmers. If it is a place where many farmers live together, then a dormitory-style house can be built. Although this type of equipment is very difficult to use in rural areas, there is such equipment in European and American rural areas, and there is no reason why dormitory-style houses cannot be applicable in our country. In addition, a public entertainment venue or meeting place should also be established in each rural village. This can both improve farmers' knowledge and provide farmers with considerable comfort, which is also essential.

In European and American rural buildings, there are usually three-bay houses, with two rooms all storage rooms, and a vacant room in the middle where cars can drive in (European and American farmers have small freight cars), which is convenient for storage, and the residence is inside, but this type of architecture is not yet applicable in our country's rural areas.
